SELECT a.*,b.value as total,c.customers_firstname as 	firstname,
	c.customers_lastname as lastname
	FROM osc_orders a inner join osc_orders_total b
	inner join osc_customers c
	WHERE a.orders_id=b.orders_id and b.class='sub_total' and a.orders_status =1 
	and c.customers_id=a.customers_id
